\subsubsection{\texorpdfstring{return\+Value}{returnValue}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily enum \hyperlink{_message_handling_8hpp_a81d556f613bfbabd0b1f9488c0fa865e}{return\+Value}}



Defines all symbols for global return values. 

The enumeration return\+Value\+Type defines all symbols for global return values. Important\+: All return values are assumed to be nonnegative!

\begin{DoxyAuthor}{Author}
Hans Joachim Ferreau 
\end{DoxyAuthor}
